   172	class Evaluation {
   173	        /** @type {Set<any>} */
   174	        values;
   175	
   176	        /**
   177	         * True if there is exactly one possible value
   178	         * @readonly
   179	         * @type {boolean}
   180	         */
   181	        is_known = true;
   182	
   183	        /**
   184	         * True if the value is known to not be null/undefined
   185	         * @readonly
   186	         * @type {boolean}
   187	         */
   188	        is_defined = true;
   189	
   190	        /**
   191	         * True if the value is known to be a string
   192	         * @readonly
   193	         * @type {boolean}
   194	         */
   195	        is_string = true;
   196	
   197	        /**
   198	         * True if the value is known to be a number
   199	         * @readonly
   200	         * @type {boolean}
   201	         */
   202	        is_number = true;
   203	
   204	        /**
   205	         * True if the value is known to be a function
   206	         * @readonly
   207	         * @type {boolean}
   208	         */
   209	        is_function = true;
   210	
   211	        /**
   212	         * @readonly
   213	         * @type {any}
   214	         */
   215	        value = undefined;
   216	
   217	        /**
   218	         *
   219	         * @param {Scope} scope
   220	         * @param {Expression | FunctionDeclaration} expression
   221	         * @param {Set<any>} values
   222	         */
   223	        constructor(scope, expression, values) {
   224	                current_evaluations.set(expression, this);
   225	
   226	                this.values = values;
   227	
   228	                switch (expression.type) {
   229	                        case 'Literal': {
   230	                                this.values.add(expression.value);
   231	                                break;
   232	                        }
   233	
   234	                        case 'Identifier': {
   235	                                const binding = scope.get(expression.name);
   236	
   237	                                if (binding) {
   238	                                        if (
   239	                                                binding.initial?.type === 'CallExpression' &&
   240	                                                get_rune(binding.initial, scope) === '$props.id'
   241	                                        ) {
   242	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   243	                                                break;
   244	                                        }
   245	
   246	                                        const is_prop =
   247	                                                binding.kind === 'prop' ||
   248	                                                binding.kind === 'rest_prop' ||
   249	                                                binding.kind === 'bindable_prop';
   250	
   251	                                        if (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' && binding.initial.index === expression.name) {
   252	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   253	                                                break;
   254	                                        }
   255	
   256	                                        if (!binding.updated && binding.initial !== null && !is_prop) {
   257	                                                binding.scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (binding.initial), this.values);
   258	                                                break;
   259	                                        }
   260	                                } else if (expression.name === 'undefined') {
   261	                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   262	                                        break;
   263	                                }
   264	
   265	                                // TODO glean what we can from reassignments
   266	                                // TODO one day, expose props and imports somehow
   267	
   268	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   269	                                break;
   270	                        }
   271	
   272	                        case 'BinaryExpression': {
   273	                                const a = scope.evaluate(/** @type {Expression} */ (expression.left)); // `left` cannot be `PrivateIdentifier` unless operator is `in`
   274	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   275	
   276	                                if (a.is_known && b.is_known) {
   277	                                        this.values.add(binary[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   278	                                        break;
   279	                                }
   280	
   281	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   282	                                        case '!=':
   283	                                        case '!==':
   284	                                        case '<':
   285	                                        case '<=':
   286	                                        case '>':
   287	                                        case '>=':
   288	                                        case '==':
   289	                                        case '===':
   290	                                        case 'in':
   291	                                        case 'instanceof':
   292	                                                this.values.add(true);
   293	                                                this.values.add(false);
   294	                                                break;
   295	
   296	                                        case '%':
   297	                                        case '&':
   298	                                        case '*':
   299	                                        case '**':
   300	                                        case '-':
   301	                                        case '/':
   302	                                        case '<<':
   303	                                        case '>>':
   304	                                        case '>>>':
   305	                                        case '^':
   306	                                        case '|':
   307	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   308	                                                break;
   309	
   310	                                        case '+':
   311	                                                if (a.is_string || b.is_string) {
   312	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   313	                                                } else if (a.is_number && b.is_number) {
   314	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   315	                                                } else {
   316	                                                        this.values.add(STRING);
   317	                                                        this.values.add(NUMBER);
   318	                                                }
   319	                                                break;
   320	
   321	                                        default:
   322	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   323	                                }
   324	                                break;
   325	                        }
   326	
   327	                        case 'ConditionalExpression': {
   328	                                const test = scope.evaluate(expression.test);
   329	                                const consequent = scope.evaluate(expression.consequent);
   330	                                const alternate = scope.evaluate(expression.alternate);
   331	
   332	                                if (test.is_known) {
   333	                                        for (const value of (test.value ? consequent : alternate).values) {
   334	                                                this.values.add(value);
   335	                                        }
   336	                                } else {
   337	                                        for (const value of consequent.values) {
   338	                                                this.values.add(value);
   339	                                        }
   340	
   341	                                        for (const value of alternate.values) {
   342	                                                this.values.add(value);
   343	                                        }
   344	                                }
   345	                                break;
   346	                        }
   347	
   348	                        case 'LogicalExpression': {
   349	                                const a = scope.evaluate(expression.left);
   350	                                const b = scope.evaluate(expression.right);
   351	
   352	                                if (a.is_known) {
   353	                                        if (b.is_known) {
   354	                                                this.values.add(logical[expression.operator](a.value, b.value));
   355	                                                break;
   356	                                        }
   357	
   358	                                        if (
   359	                                                (expression.operator === '&&' && !a.value) ||
   360	                                                (expression.operator === '||' && a.value) ||
   361	                                                (expression.operator === '??' && a.value != null)
   362	                                        ) {
   363	                                                this.values.add(a.value);
   364	                                        } else {
   365	                                                for (const value of b.values) {
   366	                                                        this.values.add(value);
   367	                                                }
   368	                                        }
   369	
   370	                                        break;
   371	                                }
   372	
   373	                                for (const value of a.values) {
   374	                                        this.values.add(value);
   375	                                }
   376	
   377	                                for (const value of b.values) {
   378	                                        this.values.add(value);
   379	                                }
   380	                                break;
   381	                        }
   382	
   383	                        case 'UnaryExpression': {
   384	                                const argument = scope.evaluate(expression.argument);
   385	
   386	                                if (argument.is_known) {
   387	                                        this.values.add(unary[expression.operator](argument.value));
   388	                                        break;
   389	                                }
   390	
   391	                                switch (expression.operator) {
   392	                                        case '!':
   393	                                        case 'delete':
   394	                                                this.values.add(false);
   395	                                                this.values.add(true);
   396	                                                break;
   397	
   398	                                        case '+':
   399	                                        case '-':
   400	                                        case '~':
   401	                                                this.values.add(NUMBER);
   402	                                                break;
   403	
   404	                                        case 'typeof':
   405	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   406	                                                break;
   407	
   408	                                        case 'void':
   409	                                                this.values.add(undefined);
   410	                                                break;
   411	
   412	                                        default:
   413	                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   414	                                }
   415	                                break;
   416	                        }
   417	
   418	                        case 'CallExpression': {
   419	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression.callee, scope);
   420	
   421	                                if (keypath) {
   422	                                        if (is_rune(keypath)) {
   423	                                                const arg = /** @type {Expression | undefined} */ (expression.arguments[0]);
   424	
   425	                                                switch (keypath) {
   426	                                                        case '$state':
   427	                                                        case '$state.raw':
   428	                                                        case '$derived':
   429	                                                                if (arg) {
   430	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg, this.values);
   431	                                                                } else {
   432	                                                                        this.values.add(undefined);
   433	                                                                }
   434	                                                                break;
   435	
   436	                                                        case '$props.id':
   437	                                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   438	                                                                break;
   439	
   440	                                                        case '$effect.tracking':
   441	                                                                this.values.add(false);
   442	                                                                this.values.add(true);
   443	                                                                break;
   444	
   445	                                                        case '$derived.by':
   446	                                                                if (arg?.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' && arg.body.type !== 'BlockStatement') {
   447	                                                                        scope.evaluate(arg.body, this.values);
   448	                                                                        break;
   449	                                                                }
   450	
   451	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   452	                                                                break;
   453	
   454	                                                        default: {
   455	                                                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   456	                                                        }
   457	                                                }
   458	
   459	                                                break;
   460	                                        }
   461	
   462	                                        if (
   463	                                                Object.hasOwn(globals, keypath) &&
   464	                                                expression.arguments.every((arg) => arg.type !== 'SpreadElement')
   465	                                        ) {
   466	                                                const [type, fn] = globals[keypath];
   467	                                                const values = expression.arguments.map((arg) => scope.evaluate(arg));
   468	
   469	                                                if (fn && values.every((e) => e.is_known)) {
   470	                                                        this.values.add(fn(...values.map((e) => e.value)));
   471	                                                } else {
   472	                                                        this.values.add(type);
   473	                                                }
   474	
   475	                                                break;
   476	                                        }
   477	                                }
   478	
   479	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   480	                                break;
   481	                        }
   482	
   483	                        case 'TemplateLiteral': {
   484	                                let result = expression.quasis[0].value.cooked;
   485	
   486	                                for (let i = 0; i < expression.expressions.length; i += 1) {
   487	                                        const e = scope.evaluate(expression.expressions[i]);
   488	
   489	                                        if (e.is_known) {
   490	                                                result += e.value + expression.quasis[i + 1].value.cooked;
   491	                                        } else {
   492	                                                this.values.add(STRING);
   493	                                                break;
   494	                                        }
   495	                                }
   496	
   497	                                this.values.add(result);
   498	                                break;
   499	                        }
   500	
   501	                        case 'MemberExpression': {
   502	                                const keypath = get_global_keypath(expression, scope);
   503	
   504	                                if (keypath && Object.hasOwn(global_constants, keypath)) {
   505	                                        this.values.add(global_constants[keypath]);
   506	                                        break;
   507	                                }
   508	
   509	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   510	                                break;
   511	                        }
   512	
   513	                        case 'ArrowFunctionExpression':
   514	                        case 'FunctionExpression':
   515	                        case 'FunctionDeclaration': {
   516	                                this.values.add(FUNCTION);
   517	                                break;
   518	                        }
   519	
   520	                        default: {
   521	                                this.values.add(UNKNOWN);
   522	                        }
   523	                }
   524	
   525	                for (const value of this.values) {
   526	                        this.value = value; // saves having special logic for `size === 1`
   527	
   528	                        if (value !== STRING && typeof value !== 'string') {
   529	                                this.is_string = false;
   530	                        }
   531	
   532	                        if (value !== NUMBER && typeof value !== 'number') {
   533	                                this.is_number = false;
   534	                        }
   535	
   536	                        if (value !== FUNCTION) {
   537	                                this.is_function = false;
   538	                        }
   539	
   540	                        if (value == null || value === UNKNOWN) {
   541	                                this.is_defined = false;
   542	                        }
   543	                }
   544	
   545	                if (this.values.size > 1 || typeof this.value === 'symbol') {
   546	                        this.is_known = false;
   547	                }
   548	
   549	                current_evaluations.delete(expression);
   550	        }
   551	}
   552	
   553	export class Scope {
   554	        /** @type {ScopeRoot} */
   555	        root;
   556	
   557	        /**
   558	         * The immediate parent scope
   559	         * @type {Scope | null}
   560	         */
   561	        parent;
   562	
   563	        /**
   564	         * Whether or not `var` declarations are contained by this scope
   565	         * @type {boolean}
   566	         */
   567	        #porous;
   568	
   569	        /**
   570	         * A map of every identifier declared by this scope, and all the
   571	         * identifiers that reference it
   572	         * @type {Map<string, Binding>}
   573	         */
   574	        declarations = new Map();
   575	
   576	        /**
   577	         * A map of declarators to the bindings they declare
   578	         * @type {Map<VariableDeclarator | AST.LetDirective, Binding[]>}
   579	         */
   580	        declarators = new Map();
   581	
   582	        /**
   583	         * A set of all the names referenced with this scope
   584	         * — useful for generating unique names
   585	         * @type {Map<string, { node: Identifier; path: AST.SvelteNode[] }[]>}
   586	         */
   587	        references = new Map();
   588	
   589	        /**
   590	         * The scope depth allows us to determine if a state variable is referenced in its own scope,
   591	         * which is usually an error. Block statements do not increase this value
   592	         */
   593	        function_depth = 0;
   594	
   595	        /**
   596	         * If tracing of reactive dependencies is enabled for this scope
   597	         * @type {null | Expression}
   598	         */
   599	        tracing = null;
   600	
   601	        /**
   602	         *
   603	         * @param {ScopeRoot} root
   604	         * @param {Scope | null} parent
   605	         * @param {boolean} porous
   606	         */
   607	        constructor(root, parent, porous) {
   608	                this.root = root;
   609	                this.parent = parent;
   610	                this.#porous = porous;
   611	                this.function_depth = parent ? parent.function_depth + (porous ? 0 : 1) : 0;
   612	        }
   613	
   614	        /**
   615	         * @param {Identifier} node
   616	         * @param {Binding['kind']} kind
   617	         * @param {DeclarationKind} declaration_kind
   618	         * @param {null | Expression | FunctionDeclaration | ClassDeclaration | ImportDeclaration | AST.EachBlock | AST.SnippetBlock} initial
   619	         * @returns {Binding}
   620	         */
   621	        declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial = null) {
   622	                if (this.parent) {
   623	                        if (declaration_kind === 'var' && this.#porous) {
   624	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind);
   625	                        }
   626	
   627	                        if (declaration_kind === 'import') {
   628	                                return this.parent.declare(node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   629	                        }
   630	                }
   631	
   632	                if (this.declarations.has(node.name)) {
   633	                        const binding = this.declarations.get(node.name);
   634	                        if (binding && binding.declaration_kind !== 'var' && declaration_kind !== 'var') {
   635	                                // This also errors on function types, but that's arguably a good thing
   636	                                // declaring function twice is also caught by acorn in the parse phase
   637	                                e.declaration_duplicate(node, node.name);
   638	                        }
   639	                }
   640	
   641	                const binding = new Binding(this, node, kind, declaration_kind, initial);
   642	
   643	                validate_identifier_name(binding, this.function_depth);
   644	
   645	                this.declarations.set(node.name, binding);
   646	                this.root.conflicts.add(node.name);
   647	                return binding;
   648	        }
   649	
   650	        child(porous = false) {
   651	                return new Scope(this.root, this, porous);
   652	        }
   653	
   654	        /**
   655	         * @param {string} preferred_name
   656	         * @returns {string}
   657	         */
   658	        generate(preferred_name) {
   659	                if (this.#porous) {
   660	                        return /** @type {Scope} */ (this.parent).generate(preferred_name);
   661	        <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   229	function get_component_name(filename) {
   230	        const parts = filename.split(/[/\\]/);
   231	        const basename = /** @type {string} */ (parts.pop());
   232	        const last_dir = /** @type {string} */ (parts.at(-1));

   235	                name = last_dir;

   242	/**
   243	 * @param {string} source

   247	export function analyze_module(source, options) {
   248	        /** @type {AST.JSComment[]} */
   249	        const comments = [];
   250

   252	        const ast = parse(source, comments, false, false);

   296	                        // and reducing the type would result in a lot of tedious type casts elsewhere - find a good solution one day
   297	                        ast_type: /** @type {any} */ (null),
   298	                        component_slots: new Set(),
   299	                        expression: null,
   300	                        function_depth: 0,
   301	                        has_props_rune: false,
   302	                        options: /** @type {ValidatedCompileOptions} */ (options),
   303	                        parent_element: null,
   304	                        reactive_statement: null
   305	                },
   306	                visitors
   307	        );
   308	
   309	        return analysis;
   310	}
   311	
   312	/**
   313	 * @param {AST.Root} root
   314	 * @param {string} source
   315	 * @param {ValidatedCompileOptions} options
   316	 * @returns {ComponentAnalysis}
   317	 */
   318	export function analyze_component(root, source, options) {
   319	        const scope_root = new ScopeRoot();
   320	
   321	        const module = js(root.module, scope_root, false, null);
   322	        const instance = js(root.instance, scope_root, true, module.scope);
   323	
   324	        const { scope, scopes, has_await } = create_scopes(
   325	                root.fragment,
   326	                scope_root,
   327	                false,
   328	                instance.scope
   329	        );
   330	
   331	        /** @type {Template} */
   332	        const template = { ast: root.fragment, scope, scopes };
   333	
   334	        let synthetic_stores_legacy_check = [];
   335	
   336	        // create synthetic bindings for store subscriptions
   337	        for (const [name, references] of module.scope.references) {
   338	                if (name[0] !== '$' || RESERVED.includes(name)) continue;
   339	                if (name === '$' || name[1] === '$') {
   340	                        e.global_reference_invalid(references[0].node, name);
   341	                }
   342	
   343	                const store_name = name.slice(1);
   344	                const declaration = instance.scope.get(store_name);
   345	                const init = /** @type {Node | undefined} */ (declaration?.initial);
   346	
   347	                // If we're not in legacy mode through the compiler option, assume the user
   348	                // is referencing a rune and not a global store.
   349	                if (
   350	                        options.runes === false ||
   351	                        !is_rune(name) ||
   352	                        (declaration !== null &&
   353	                                // const state = $state(0) is valid
   354	                                (get_rune(init, instance.scope) === null ||
   355	                                        // rune-line names received as props are valid too (but we have to protect against $props as store)
   356	                                        (store_name !== 'props' && get_rune(init, instance.scope) === '$props')) &&
   357	                                // allow `import { derived } from 'svelte/store'` in the same file as `const x = $derived(..)` because one is not a subscription to the other
   358	                                !(
   359	                                        name === '$derived' &&
   360	                                        declaration.initial?.type === 'ImportDeclaration' &&
   361	                                        declaration.initial.source.value === 'svelte/store'
   362	                                ))
   363	                ) {
   364	                        let is_nested_store_subscription_node = undefined;
   365	                        search: for (const reference of references) {
   366	                                for (let i = reference.path.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   367	                                        const scope =
   368	                                                scopes.get(reference.path[i]) ||
   369	                                                module.scopes.get(reference.path[i]) ||
   370	                                                instance.scopes.get(reference.path[i]);
   371	                                        if (scope) {
   372	                                                const owner = scope?.owner(store_name);
   373	                                                if (!!owner && owner !== module.scope && owner !== instance.scope) {
   374	                                                        is_nested_store_subscription_node = reference.node;
   375	                                                        break search;
   376	                                                }
   377	                                                break;
   378	                                        }
   379	                                }
   380	                        }
   381	
   382	                        if (is_nested_store_subscription_node) {
   383	                                e.store_invalid_scoped_subscription(is_nested_store_subscription_node);
   384	                        }
   385	
   386	                        if (options.runes !== false) {
   387	                                if (declaration === null && /[a-z]/.test(store_name[0])) {
   388	                                        e.global_reference_invalid(references[0].node, name);
   389	                                } else if (declaration !== null && is_rune(name)) {
   390	                                        for (const { node, path } of references) {
   391	                                                if (path.at(-1)?.type === 'CallExpression') {
   392	                                                        w.store_rune_conflict(node, store_name);
   393	                                                }
   394	                                        }
   395	                                }
   396	                        }
   397	
   398	                        if (module.ast) {
   399	                                for (const { node, path } of references) {
   400	                                        // if the reference is inside module, error. this is a bit hacky but it works
   401	                                        if (
   402	                                                /** @type {number} */ (node.start) > /** @type {number} */ (module.ast.start) &&
   403	                                                /** @type {number} */ (node.end) < /** @type {number} */ (module.ast.end) &&
   404	                                                // const state = $state(0) is valid
   405	                                                get_rune(/** @type {Node} */ (path.at(-1)), module.scope) === null
   406	                                        ) {
   407	                                                e.store_invalid_subscription(node);
   408	                                        }
   409	                                }
   410	                        }
   411	
   412	                        // we push to the array because at this moment in time we can't be sure if we are in legacy
   413	                        // mode yet because we are still changing the module scope
   414	                        synthetic_stores_legacy_check.push(() => {
   415	                                // if we are creating a synthetic binding for a let declaration we should also declare
   416	                                // the declaration as state in case it's reassigned and we are not in runes mode (the function will
   417	                                // not be called if we are not in runes mode, that's why there's no !runes check here)
   418	                                if (
   419	                                        declaration !== null &&
   420	                                        declaration.kind === 'normal' &&
   421	                                        declaration.declaration_kind === 'let' &&
   422	                                        declaration.reassigned
   423	                                ) {
   424	                                        declaration.kind = 'state';
   425	                                }
   426	                        });
   427	
   428	                        const binding = instance.scope.declare(b.id(name), 'store_sub', 'synthetic');
   429	                        binding.references = references;
   430	                        instance.scope.references.set(name, references);
   431	                        module.scope.references.delete(name);
   432	                }
   433	        }
   434	
   435	        const component_name = get_component_name(options.filename);
   436	
   437	        const runes =
   438	                options.runes ??
   439	                (has_await || instance.has_await || Array.from(module.scope.references.keys()).some(is_rune));
   440	
   441	        if (!runes) {
   442	                for (let check of synthetic_stores_legacy_check) {
   443	                        check();
   444	                }
   445	        }
   446	
   447	        if (runes && root.module) {
   448	                const context = root.module.attributes.find((attribute) => attribute.name === 'context');
   449	                if (context) {
   450	                        w.script_context_deprecated(context);
   451	                }
   452	        }
   453	
   454	        // TODO remove all the ?? stuff, we don't need it now that we're validating the config
   455	        /** @type {ComponentAnalysis} */
   456	        const analysis = {
   457	                name: module.scope.generate(options.name ?? component_name),
   458	                root: scope_root,
   459	                module,
   460	                instance,
   461	                template,
   462	                comments: root.comments,
   463	                elements: [],
   464	                runes,
   465	                // if we are not in runes mode but we have no reserved references ($$props, $$restProps)
   466	                // and no `export let` we might be in a wannabe runes component that is using runes in an external
   467	                // module...we need to fallback to the runic behavior
   468	                maybe_runes:
   469	                        !runes &&
   470	                        // if they explicitly disabled runes, use the legacy behavior
   471	                        options.runes !== false &&
   472	                        ![...module.scope.references.keys()].some((name) =>
   473	                                ['$$props', '$$restProps'].includes(name)
   474	                        ) &&
   475	                        !instance.ast.body.some(
   476	                                (node) =>
   477	                                        node.type === 'LabeledStatement' ||
   478	                                        (node.type === 'ExportNamedDeclaration' &&
   479	                                                ((node.declaration &&
   480	                                                        node.declaration.type === 'VariableDeclaration' &&
   481	                                                        node.declaration.kind === 'let') ||
   482	                                                        node.specifiers.some(
   483	                                                                (specifier) =>
   484	                                                                        specifier.local.type === 'Identifier' &&
   485	                                                                        instance.scope.get(specifier.local.name)?.declaration_kind === 'let'
   486	                                                        )))
   487	                        ),
   488	                tracing: false,
   489	                classes: new Map(),
   490	                immutable: runes || options.immutabl<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.    147	                                        if (
   148	                                                element.type !== 'RegularElement' ||
   149	                                                element.metadata.has_spread ||
   150	                                                !is_delegated(event_name)
   151	                                        ) {
   152	                                                return unhoisted;
   153	                                        }
   154	                                } else if (parent.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' && parent.type !== 'VariableDeclarator') {
   155	                                        return unhoisted;
   156	                                }
   157	                        }
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                // If the binding is exported, bail out
   161	                if (context.state.analysis.exports.find((node) => node.name === handler.name)) {
   162	                        return unhoisted;
   163	                }
   164	
   165	                if (binding?.is_function()) {
   166	                        target_function = binding.initial;
   167	                }
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        // If we can't find a function, or the function has multiple parameters, bail out
   171	        if (target_function == null || target_function.params.length > 1) {
   172	                return unhoisted;
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        const visited_references = new Set();
   176	        const scope = target_function.metadata.scope;
   177	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
   178	                // Bail out if the arguments keyword is used or $host is referenced
   179	                if (reference === 'arguments' || reference === '$host') return unhoisted;
   180	                // Bail out if references a store subscription
   181	                if (scope.get(`$${reference}`)?.kind === 'store_sub') return unhoisted;
   182	
   183	                const binding = scope.get(reference);
   184	                const local_binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
   185	
   186	                // if the function access a snippet that can't be hoisted we bail out
   187	                if (
   188	                        local_binding !== null &&
   189	                        local_binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock' &&
   190	                        !local_binding.initial.metadata.can_hoist
   191	                ) {
   192	                        return unhoisted;
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                // If we are referencing a binding that is shadowed in another scope then bail out.
   196	                if (local_binding !== null && binding !== null && local_binding.node !== binding.node) {
   197	                        return unhoisted;
   198	                }
   199	
   200	                // If we have multiple references to the same store using $ prefix, bail out.
   201	                if (
   202	                        binding !== null &&
   203	                        binding.kind === 'store_sub' &&
   204	                        visited_references.has(reference.slice(1))
   205	                ) {
   206	                        return unhoisted;
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we reference the index within an each block, then bail out.
   210	                if (binding !== null && binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' && binding.node.name === binding.initial.index) return unhoisted;
   211	
   212	                if (
   213	                        binding !== null &&
   214	                        // Bail out if the binding is a rest param
   215	                        (binding.declaration_kind === 'rest_param' ||
   216	                                // Bail out if we reference anything from the EachBlock (for now) that mutates in non-runes mode,
   217	                                (((!context.state.analysis.runes && binding.kind === 'each') ||
   218	                                        // or any normal not reactive bindings that are mutated.
   219	                                        binding.kind === 'normal') &&
   220	                                        binding.updated))
   221	                ) {
   222	                        return unhoisted;
   223	                }
   224	                visited_references.add(reference);
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        return { hoisted: true, function: target_function };
   228	}
   229	
   230	/**
   231	 * @param {string} event_name
   232	 */
   233	function get_attribute_event_name(event_name) {
   234	        event_name = event_name.slice(2);
   235	        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
   236	                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
   237	        }
   238	        return event_name;
   239	}
   240

    76	                        }

    81	/** @type {DelegatedEvent} */
    82	const unhoisted = { hoisted: false };
    83	
    84	/**
    85	 * Checks if given event attribute can be delegated/hoisted and returns the corresponding info if so
    86	 * @param {string} event_name
    87	 * @param {Expression | null} handler
    88	 * @param {Context} context
    89	 * @returns {null | DelegatedEvent}
    90	 */
    91	function get_delegated_event(event_name, handler, context) {
    92	        // Handle delegated event handlers. Bail out if not a delegated event.
    93	        if (!handler || !is_delegated(event_name)) {
    94	                return null;
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        // If we are not working with a RegularElement, then bail out.
    98	        const element = context.path.at(-1);
    99	        if (element?.type !== 'RegularElement') {
   100	                return null;
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        /** @type {FunctionExpression | FunctionDeclaration | ArrowFunctionExpression | null} */
   104	        let target_function = null;
   105	        let binding = null;
   106	
   107	        if (element.metadata.has_spread) {
   108	                // event attribute becomes part of the dynamic spread array
   109	                return unhoisted;
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if (handler.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' || handler.type === 'FunctionExpression') {
   113	                target_function = handler;
   114	        } else if (handler.type === 'Identifier') {
   115	                binding = context.state.scope.get(handler.name);
   116	
   117	                if (context.state.analysis.module.scope.references.has(handler.name)) {
   118	                        // If a binding with the same name is referenced in the module scope (even if not declared there), bail out
   119	                        return unhoisted;
   120	                }
   121	
   122	                if (binding != null) {
   123	                        for (const { path } of binding.references) {
   124	                                const parent = path.at(-1);
   125	                                if (parent === undefined) return unhoisted;
   126	
   127	                                const grandparent = path.at(-2);
   128	
   129	                                /** @type {AST.RegularElement | null} */
   130	                                let element = null;
   131	                                /** @type {string | null} */
   132	                                let event_name = null;
   133	                                if (parent.type === 'OnDirective') {
   134	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (grandparent);
   135	                                        event_name = parent.name;
   136	                                } else if (
   137	                                        parent.type === 'ExpressionTag' &&
   138	                                        grandparent?.type === 'Attribute' &&
   139	                                        is_event_attribute(grandparent)
   140	                                ) {
   141	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (path.at(-3));
   142	                                        const attribute = /** @type {AST.Attribute} */ (grandparent);
   143	                                        event_name = get_attribute_event_name(attribute.name);
   144	                                }
   145	
   146	                                if (element && event_name) {
   147	                                        if (
   148	                                                element.type !== 'RegularElement' ||
   149	                                                element.metadata.has_spread ||
   150	                                                !is_delegated(event_name)
   151	                                        ) {
   152	                                                return unhoisted;
   153	                                        }
   154	                                } else if (parent.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' && parent.type !== 'VariableDeclarator') {
   155	                                        return unhoisted;
   156	                                }
   157	                        }
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                // If the binding is exported, bail out
   161	                if (context.state.analysis.exports.find((node) => node.name === handler.name)) {
   162	                        return unhoisted;
   163	                }
   164	
   165	                if (binding?.is_function()) {
   166	                        target_function = binding.initial;
   167	                }
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        // If we can't find a function, or the function has multiple parameters, bail out
   171	        if (target_function == null || target_function.params.length > 1) {
   172	                return unhoisted;
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        const visited_references = new Set();
   176	        const scope = target_function.metadata.scope;
   177	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
   178	                // Bail out if the arguments keyword is used or $host is referenced
   179	                if (reference === 'arguments' || reference === '$host') return unhoisted;
   180	                // Bail out if references a store subscription
   181	                if (scope.get(`$${reference}`)?.kind === 'store_sub') return unhoisted;
   182	
   183	                const binding = scope.get(reference);
   184	                const local_binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
   185	
   186	                // if the function access a snippet that can't be hoisted we bail out
   187	                if (
   188	                        local_binding !== null &&
   189	                        local_binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock' &&
   190	                        !local_binding.initial.metadata.can_hoist
   191	                ) {
   192	                        return unhoisted;
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                // If we are referencing a binding that is shadowed in another scope then bail out.
   196	                if (local_binding !== null && binding !== null && local_binding.node !== binding.node) {
   197	                        return unhoisted;
   198	                }
   199	
   200	                // If we have multiple references to the same store using $ prefix, bail out.
   201	                if (
   202	                        binding !== null &&
   203	                        binding.kind === 'store_sub' &&
   204	                        visited_references.has(reference.slice(1))
   205	                ) {
   206	                        return unhoisted;
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we reference the index within an each block, then bail out.
   210	                if (binding !== null && binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock') return unhoisted;
   211	
   212	                if (
   213	                        binding !== null &&
   214	                        // Bail out if the binding is a rest param
   215	                        (binding.declaration_kind === 'rest_param' ||
   216	                                // Bail out if we reference anything from the EachBlock (for now) that mutates in non-runes mode,
   217	                                (((!context.state.analysis.runes && binding.kind === 'each') ||
   218	                                        // or any normal not reactive bindings that are mutated.
   219	                                        binding.kind === 'normal') &&
   220	                                        binding.updated))
   221	                ) {
   222	                        return unhoisted;
   223	                }
   224	                visited_references.add(reference);
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        return { hoisted: true, function: target_function };
   228	}

    13	 * @param {AST.Attribute} node

    16	export function Attribute(node, context) {
    17	        context.next();
    18	
    19	        const parent = /** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (context.path.at(-1));
    20	
    21	        if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
    22	                // special case <option value="" />
    23	                if (node.name === 'value' && parent.name === 'option') {
    24	                        mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    25	                }
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        if (is_event_attribute(node)) {
    29	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (cannot_be_set_statically(node.name)) {
    33	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        // class={[...]} or class={{...}} or `class={x}` need clsx to resolve the classes
    37	        if (
    38	                node.name === 'class' &&
    39	                !Array.isArray(node.value) &&
    40	                node.value !== true &&
    41	                node.value.expression.type !== 'Literal' &&
    42	                node.value.expression.type !== 'TemplateLiteral' &&
    43	                node.value.expression.type !== 'BinaryExpression'
    44	        ) {
    45	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    46	                node.metadata.needs_clsx = true;

    48

    51	                        if (chunk.type !== 'ExpressionTag') continue;
    52	
    53	                        if (

    55	                                chunk.expression.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression'
    56	                        ) {
    57	                                continue;
    58	                        }
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if (is_event_attribute(node)) {
    62	                        const parent = context.path.at(-1);
    63	                        if (parent?.type === 'RegularElement' || parent?.type === 'SvelteElement') {
    64	                                context.state.analysis.uses_event_attributes = true;
    65	                        }
    66	
    67	                        const expression = get_attribute_expression(node);
    68	                        const delegated_event = get_delegated_event(node.name.slice(2), expression, context);
    69	
    70	                        if (delegated_event !== null) {
    71	                                if (delegated_event.hoisted) {
    72	                                        delegated_event.function.metadata.hoisted = true;
    73	                                }
    74	
    75	                                node.metadata.delegated = delegated_event;
    76	                        }
    77	                }
    78	        }
    79	}
    80	
    81	/** @type {DelegatedEvent} */
    82	const unhoisted = { hoisted: false };
    83	
    84	/**
    85	 * Checks if given event attribute can be delegated/hoisted and returns the corresponding info if so
    86	 * @param {string} event_name
    87	 * @param {Expression | null} handler
    88	 * @param {Context} context
    89	 * @returns {null | DelegatedEvent}
    90	 */
    91	function get_delegated_event(event_name, handler, context) {
    92	        // Handle delegated event handlers. Bail out if not a delegated event.
    93	        if (!handler || !is_delegated(event_name)) {
    94	                return null;
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        // If we are not working with a RegularElement, then bail out.
    98	        const element = context.path.at(-1);
    99	        if (element?.type !== 'RegularElement') {
   100	                return null;
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        /** @type {FunctionExpression | FunctionDeclaration | ArrowFunctionExpression | null} */
   104	        let target_function = null;
   105	        let binding = null;
   106	
   107	        if (element.metadata.has_spread) {
   108	                // event attribute becomes part of the dynamic spread array
   109	                return unhoisted;
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if (handler.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' || handler.type === 'FunctionExpression') {
   113	                target_function = handler;
   114	        } else if (handler.type === 'Identifier') {
   115	                binding = context.state.scope.get(handler.name);
   116	
   117	                if (context.state.analysis.module.scope.references.has(handler.name)) {
   118	                        // If a binding with the same name is referenced in the module scope (even if not declared there), bail out
   119	                        return unhoisted;
   120	                }
   121	
   122	                if (binding != null) {
   123	                        for (const { path } of binding.references) {
   124	                                const parent = path.at(-1);
   125	                                if (parent === undefined) return unhoisted;
   126	
   127	                                const grandparent = path.at(-2);
   128	
   129	                                /** @type {AST.RegularElement | null} */
   130	                                let element = null;
   131	                                /** @type {string | null} */
   132	                                let event_name = null;
   133	                                if (parent.type === 'OnDirective') {
   134	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (grandparent);
   135	                                        event_name = parent.name;
   136	                                } else if (
   137	                                        parent.type === 'ExpressionTag' &&
   138	                                        grandparent?.type === 'Attribute' &&
   139	                                        is_event_attribute(grandparent)
   140	                                ) {
   141	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (path.at(-3));
   142	                                        const attribute = /** @type {AST.Attribute} */ (grandparent);
   143	                                        event_name = get_attribute_event_name(attribute.name);
   144	                                }
   145	
   146	                                if (element && event_name) {
   147	                                        if (
   148	                                                element.type !== 'RegularElement' ||
   149	                                                element.metadata.has_spread ||
   150	                                                !is_delegated(event_name)
   151	                                        ) {
   152	                                                return unhoisted;
   153	                                        }
   154	                                } else if (parent.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' && parent.type !== 'VariableDeclarator') {
   155	                                        return unhoisted;
   156	                                }
   157	                        }
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                // If the binding is exported, bail out
   161	                if (context.state.analysis.exports.find((node) => node.name === handler.name)) {
   162	                        return unhoisted;
   163	                }
   164	
   165	                if (binding?.is_function()) {
   166	                        target_function = binding.initial;
   167	                }
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        // If we can't find a function, or the function has multiple parameters, bail out
   171	        if (target_function == null || target_function.params.length > 1) {
   172	                return unhoisted;
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        const visited_references = new Set();
   176	        const scope = target_function.metadata.scope;
   177	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
   178	                // Bail out if the arguments keyword is used or $host is referenced
   179	                if (reference === 'arguments' || reference === '$host') return unhoisted;
   180	                // Bail out if references a store subscription
   181	                if (scope.get(`$${reference}`)?.kind === 'store_sub') return unhoisted;
   182	
   183	                const binding = scope.get(reference);
   184	                const local_binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
   185	
   186	                // if the function access a snippet that can't be hoisted we bail out
   187	                if (
   188	                        local_binding !== null &&
   189	                        local_binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock' &&
   190	                        !local_binding.initial.metadata.can_hoist
   191	                ) {
   192	                        return unhoisted;
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                // If we are referencing a binding that is shadowed in another scope then bail out.
   196	                if (local_binding !== null && binding !== null && local_binding.node !== binding.node) {
   197	                        return unhoisted;
   198	                }
   199	
   200	                // If we have multiple references to the same store using $ prefix, bail out.
   201	                if (
   202	                        binding !== null &&
   203	                        binding.kind === 'store_sub' &&
   204	                        visited_references.has(reference.slice(1))
   205	                ) {
   206	                        return unhoisted;
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we reference the index within an each block, then bail out.
   210	                if (binding !== null && (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' || binding.kind === 'each')) {
   211	                        if (local_binding === null || local_binding.node === binding.node) {
   212	                                return unhoisted;
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                if (
   217	                        binding !== null &&
   218	                        // Bail out if the binding is a rest param
   219	                        (binding.declaration_kind === 'rest_param' ||
   220	                                // Bail out if we reference anything from the EachBlock (for now) that mutates in non-runes mode,
   221	                                (((!context.state.analysis.runes && binding.kind === 'each') ||
   222	                                        // or any normal not reactive bindings that are mutated.
   223	                                        binding.kind === 'normal') &&
   224	                                        binding.updated))
   225	                ) {
   226	                        return unhoisted;
   227	                }
   228	                visited_references.add(reference);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        return { hoisted: true, function: target_function };
   232	}
   233	
   234	/**
   235	 * @param {string} event_name
   236	 */
   237	function get_attribute_event_name(event_name) {
   238	        event_name = event_name.slice(2);
   239	        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
   240	                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
   241	        }
   242	        return event_name;
   243	}

     5	import {
     6	        get_attribute_chunks,
     7	        get_attribute_expression,
     8	        is_event_attribute
     9	} from '../../../utils/ast.js';
    10	import { mark_subtree_dynamic } from './shared/fragment.js';
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * @param {AST.Attribute} node
    14	 * @param {Context} context
    15	 */
    16	export function Attribute(node, context) {
    17	        context.next();
    18	
    19	        const parent = /** @type {AST.SvelteNode} */ (context.path.at(-1));
    20	
    21	        if (parent.type === 'RegularElement') {
    22	                // special case <option value="" />
    23	                if (node.name === 'value' && parent.name === 'option') {
    24	                        mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    25	                }
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        if (is_event_attribute(node)) {
    29	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (cannot_be_set_statically(node.name)) {
    33	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        // class={[...]} or class={{...}} or `class={x}` need clsx to resolve the classes
    37	        if (
    38	                node.name === 'class' &&
    39	                !Array.isArray(node.value) &&
    40	                node.value !== true &&
    41	                node.value.expression.type !== 'Literal' &&
    42	                node.value.expression.type !== 'TemplateLiteral' &&
    43	                node.value.expression.type !== 'BinaryExpression'
    44	        ) {
    45	                mark_subtree_dynamic(context.path);
    46	                node.metadata.needs_clsx = true;
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        if (node.value !== true) {
    50	                for (const chunk of get_attribute_chunks(node.value)) {
    51	                        if (chunk.type !== 'ExpressionTag') continue;
    52	
    53	                        if (
    54	                                chunk.expression.type === 'FunctionExpression' ||
    55	                                chunk.expression.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression'
    56	                        ) {
    57	                                continue;
    58	                        }
    59	                }
    60	
    61	                if (is_event_attribute(node)) {
    62	                        const parent = context.path.at(-1);
    63	                        if (parent?.type === 'RegularElement' || parent?.type === 'SvelteElement') {
    64	                                context.state.analysis.uses_event_attributes = true;
    65	                        }
    66	
    67	                        const expression = get_attribute_expression(node);
    68	                        const delegated_event = get_delegated_event(node.name.slice(2), expression, context);
    69	
    70	                        if (delegated_event !== null) {
    71	                                if (delegated_event.hoisted) {
    72	                                        delegated_event.function.metadata.hoisted = true;
    73	                                }
    74	
    75	                                node.metadata.delegated = delegated_event;
    76	                        }
    77	                }
    78	        }
    79	}
    80	
    81	/** @type {DelegatedEvent} */
    82	const unhoisted = { hoisted: false };
    83	
    84	/**
    85	 * Checks if given event attribute can be delegated/hoisted and returns the corresponding info if so
    86	 * @param {string} event_name
    87	 * @param {Expression | null} handler
    88	 * @param {Context} context
    89	 * @returns {null | DelegatedEvent}
    90	 */
    91	function get_delegated_event(event_name, handler, context) {
    92	        // Handle delegated event handlers. Bail out if not a delegated event.
    93	        if (!handler || !is_delegated(event_name)) {
    94	                return null;
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        // If we are not working with a RegularElement, then bail out.
    98	        const element = context.path.at(-1);
    99	        if (element?.type !== 'RegularElement') {
   100	                return null;
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        /** @type {FunctionExpression | FunctionDeclaration | ArrowFunctionExpression | null} */
   104	        let target_function = null;
   105	        let binding = null;
   106	
   107	        if (element.metadata.has_spread) {
   108	                // event attribute becomes part of the dynamic spread array
   109	                return unhoisted;
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        if (handler.type === 'ArrowFunctionExpression' || handler.type === 'FunctionExpression') {
   113	                target_function = handler;
   114	        } else if (handler.type === 'Identifier') {
   115	                binding = context.state.scope.get(handler.name);
   116	
   117	                if (context.state.analysis.module.scope.references.has(handler.name)) {
   118	                        // If a binding with the same name is referenced in the module scope (even if not declared there), bail out
   119	                        return unhoisted;
   120	                }
   121	
   122	                if (binding != null) {
   123	                        for (const { path } of binding.references) {
   124	                                const parent = path.at(-1);
   125	                                if (parent === undefined) return unhoisted;
   126	
   127	                                const grandparent = path.at(-2);
   128	
   129	                                /** @type {AST.RegularElement | null} */
   130	                                let element = null;
   131	                                /** @type {string | null} */
   132	                                let event_name = null;
   133	                                if (parent.type === 'OnDirective') {
   134	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (grandparent);
   135	                                        event_name = parent.name;
   136	                                } else if (
   137	                                        parent.type === 'ExpressionTag' &&
   138	                                        grandparent?.type === 'Attribute' &&
   139	                                        is_event_attribute(grandparent)
   140	                                ) {
   141	                                        element = /** @type {AST.RegularElement} */ (path.at(-3));
   142	                                        const attribute = /** @type {AST.Attribute} */ (grandparent);
   143	                                        event_name = get_attribute_event_name(attribute.name);
   144	                                }
   145	
   146	                                if (element && event_name) {
   147	                                        if (
   148	                                                element.type !== 'RegularElement' ||
   149	                                                element.metadata.has_spread ||
   150	                                                !is_delegated(event_name)
   151	                                        ) {
   152	                                                return unhoisted;
   153	                                        }
   154	                                } else if (parent.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' && parent.type !== 'VariableDeclarator') {
   155	                                        return unhoisted;
   156	                                }
   157	                        }
   158	                }
   159	
   160	                // If the binding is exported, bail out
   161	                if (context.state.analysis.exports.find((node) => node.name === handler.name)) {
   162	                        return unhoisted;
   163	                }
   164	
   165	                if (binding?.is_function()) {
   166	                        target_function = binding.initial;
   167	                }
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        // If we can't find a function, or the function has multiple parameters, bail out
   171	        if (target_function == null || target_function.params.length > 1) {
   172	                return unhoisted;
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        const visited_references = new Set();
   176	        const scope = target_function.metadata.scope;
   177	        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
   178	                // Bail out if the arguments keyword is used or $host is referenced
   179	                if (reference === 'arguments' || reference === '$host') return unhoisted;
   180	                // Bail out if references a store subscription
   181	                if (scope.get(`$${reference}`)?.kind === 'store_sub') return unhoisted;
   182	
   183	                const binding = scope.get(reference);
   184	                const local_binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
   185	
   186	                // if the function access a snippet that can't be hoisted we bail out
   187	                if (
   188	                        local_binding !== null &&
   189	                        local_binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock' &&
   190	                        !local_binding.initial.metadata.can_hoist
   191	                ) {
   192	                        return unhoisted;
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                // If we are referencing a binding that is shadowed in another scope then bail out.
   196	                if (local_binding !== null && binding !== null && local_binding.node !== binding.node) {
   197	                        return unhoisted;
   198	                }
   199	
   200	                // If we have multiple references to the same store using $ prefix, bail out.
   201	                if (
   202	                        binding !== null &&
   203	                        binding.kind === 'store_sub' &&
   204	                        visited_references.has(reference.slice(1))
   205	                ) {
   206	                        return unhoisted;
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we reference the index within an each block, then bail out.
   210	                if (binding !== null && (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' || binding.kind === 'each')) {
   211	                        if (local_binding === null || local_binding.node === binding.node) {
   212	                                return unhoisted;
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                if (
   217	                        binding !== null &&
   218	                        // Bail out if the binding is a rest param
   219	                        (binding.declaration_kind === 'rest_param' ||
   220	                                // Bail out if we reference anything from the EachBlock (for now) that mutates in non-runes mode,
   221	                                (((!context.state.analysis.runes && binding.kind === 'each') ||
   222	                                        // or any normal not reactive bindings that are mutated.
   223	                                        binding.kind === 'normal') &&
   224	                                        binding.updated))
   225	                ) {
   226	                        return unhoisted;
   227	                }
   228	                visited_references.add(reference);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        return { hoisted: true, function: target_function };
   232	}
   233	
   234	/**
   235	 * @param {string} event_name
   236	 */
   237	function get_attribute_event_name(event_name) {
   238	        event_name = event_name.slice(2);
   239	        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
   240	                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
   241	        }
   242	        return event_name;
   243	}
   244

+                                        const attribute = /** @type {AST.Attribute} */ (grandparent);
+                                        event_name = get_attribute_event_name(attribute.name);
+                                }
+
+                                if (element && event_name) {
+                                        if (
+                                                element.type !== 'RegularElement' ||
+                                                element.metadata.has_spread ||
+                                                !is_delegated(event_name)
+                                        ) {
+                                                return unhoisted;
+                                        }
+                                } else if (parent.type !== 'FunctionDeclaration' && parent.type !== 'VariableDeclarator') {
+                                        return unhoisted;
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // If the binding is exported, bail out
+                if (context.state.analysis.exports.find((node) => node.name === handler.name)) {
+                        return unhoisted;
+                }
+
+                if (binding?.is_function()) {
+                        target_function = binding.initial;
+                }
+        }
+
+        // If we can't find a function, or the function has multiple parameters, bail out
+        if (target_function == null || target_function.params.length > 1) {
+                return unhoisted;
+        }
+
+        const visited_references = new Set();
+        const scope = target_function.metadata.scope;
+        for (const [reference] of scope.references) {
+                // Bail out if the arguments keyword is used or $host is referenced
+                if (reference === 'arguments' || reference === '$host') return unhoisted;
+                // Bail out if references a store subscription
+                if (scope.get(`$${reference}`)?.kind === 'store_sub') return unhoisted;
+
+                const binding = scope.get(reference);
+                const local_binding = context.state.scope.get(reference);
+
+                // if the function access a snippet that can't be hoisted we bail out
+                if (
+                        local_binding !== null &&
+                        local_binding.initial?.type === 'SnippetBlock' &&
+                        !local_binding.initial.metadata.can_hoist
+                ) {
+                        return unhoisted;
+                }
+
+                // If we are referencing a binding that is shadowed in another scope then bail out.
+                if (local_binding !== null && binding !== null && local_binding.node !== binding.node) {
+                        return unhoisted;
+                }
+
+                // If we have multiple references to the same store using $ prefix, bail out.
+                if (
+                        binding !== null &&
+                        binding.kind === 'store_sub' &&
+                        visited_references.has(reference.slice(1))
+                ) {
+                        return unhoisted;
+                }
+
+                // If we reference the index within an each block, then bail out.
+                if (binding !== null && (binding.initial?.type === 'EachBlock' || binding.kind === 'each')) {
+                        if (local_binding === null || local_binding.node === binding.node) {
+                                return unhoisted;
+                        }
+                }
+
+                if (
+                        binding !== null &&
+                        // Bail out if the binding is a rest param
+                        (binding.declaration_kind === 'rest_param' ||
+                                // Bail out if we reference anything from the EachBlock (for now) that mutates in non-runes mode,
+                                (((!context.state.analysis.runes && binding.kind === 'each') ||
+                                        // or any normal not reactive bindings that are mutated.
+                                        binding.kind === 'normal') &&
+                                        binding.updated))
+                ) {
+                        return unhoisted;
+                }
+                visited_references.add(reference);
+        }
+
+        return { hoisted: true, function: target_function };
 }
